# Chunk read order (by source line)

Chunk files are named `blk_<hash>.md`. **Lexical sort of filenames is not document order.**
Open chunks in this sequence (or sort `context_index.json` `blocks[]` by `source_anchor.line_start`).
The **chunk_id** column links to each `chunks/*.md` file.
